border-purple-500/20 bg-purple-500/5',\n    activeClasses: 'text-white border-purple-400/40 bg-purple-500/10 ring-2 ring-purple-400/30',\n    features: [\n      'Tout Premium +',\n      'Badge \"Elite 'text-green-400' : s >= 50 ? 'text-yellow-400' : s >= 30 ? 'text-orange-400' : 'text-red-400';\nconst getScoreBg = (s: number) => s >= 70 ? 'bg-green-500' : s >= 50 ? 'bg-yellow-500' : s >= 30 ? 'bg-orange-500' : 'bg-red-500';\n\nconst Directory: React.FC<DirectoryProps> = ({ onBack, onViewEntity, onNavigateToPlan, user, directClientCount, maxClients }) => {\n  const [viewMode, setViewMode] = useState<'browse' | 'join'>('browse');\n  const [joinStep, setJoinStep] = useState<'form' | 'audit' | 'plan' | 'payment' | 'success'>('form');\n  const [searchTerm, setSearchTerm] = useState('');\n  const [selectedFilter, setSelectedFilter] = useState('All');\n  const [showLimitAlert, setShowLimitAlert] = useState(false);\n  const [isAuditing, setIsAuditing] = useState(false);\n  const [auditScore, setAuditScore] = useState<number | null>(null);\n  const [auditProgress, setAuditProgress] = useState(0);\n  const [isProcessingPayment, setIsProcessingPayment] = useState(false);\n\n  const isAtLimit = directClientCount >= maxClients && user?.plan !== 'enterprise';\n  const planLabel = user?.plan === 'free' ? 'premium' : 'standard';\n\n  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({\n    companyName: '',\n    website: '',\n    sector: '',\n    description: '',\n    contactName: user?.name || '',\n    contactEmail: user?.email || '',\n  });\n\n  const handleJoinIndex = () => {\n    if (isAtLimit) {\n      setShowLimitAlert(true);\n      return;\n    }\n    setViewMode('join');\n    setJoinStep('form');\n    setAuditScore(null);\n    setAuditProgress(0);\n  };\n\n  const handleInputChange = (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement | HTMLSelectElement>) => {\n    setFormData({ ...formData, [e.target.name]: e.target.value });\n  };\n\n  const handleFormSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {\n    e.preventDefault();\n    setJoinStep('audit');\n    runAudit();\n  };\n\n  const runAudit = () => {\n    setIsAuditing(true);\n    setAuditProgress(0);\n    // Simulate audit progress\n    const interval = setInterval(() => {\n      setAuditProgress(prev => {\n        if (prev >= 100) {\n          clearInterval(interval);\n          return 100;\n        }\n        return prev + Math.random() * 15 + 5;\n      });\n    }, 400);\n\n    setTimeout(() => {\n      clearInterval(interval);\n      setAuditProgress(100);\n      const score = Math.floor(Math.random() * 45) + 20; 'success' : 'warning', message: isElite ? 'Page \"À propos\" détaillée' : 'Page \"À propos\" perfectible' }] },\n      semantic: { name: \"Structure Sémantique\", score: score - 5, weight: 10, items: [{ status: 'success', message: 'Balisage Schema.org Organization valide' }, { status: 'success', message: 'Structure Hn logique' }] },\n      content: { name: \"Profondeur Contenu\", score: score - 2, weight: 10, items: [{ status: 'success', message: 'Densité entités nommées élevée' }] },\n    };\n    return {\n      url, timestamp: new Date().toISOString(), globalScore: score, categories, recommendations: [],\n      aiCitation: { before: `Je n'ai pas d'informations précises sur ${item.name}.`, after: `D'après ses données structurées, ${item.name} est un leader en ${item.sector}.`, probability: Math.max(score - 10, 50) }\n    };\n  };\n\n  const handleViewDetails = (item: typeof DIRECTORY_DATA[0]) => {\n    onViewEntity(generateMockAnalysis(item));\n  };\n\n  // =============================================\n  // BROWSER VIEW\n  // =============================================\n  const renderBrowser = () => (\n    <div className=\"space-y-8 animate-in fade-in duration-500\">\n      <div className=\"text-center space-y-4 mb-12\">\n        <h1 className=\"text-4xl md:text-5xl font-sans font-bold text-white\">\n          Annuaire <span className=\"text-purple-400 italic\">Knowledge Graph</span>\n        </h1>\n        <p className=\"text-gray-500 text-lg max-w-2xl mx-auto\">\n          Explorez les entités certifiées AEO. 'text-white' : 'text-gray-600'}`}>{s.label}</span>\n                </div>\n                {i < steps.length - 1 && <div className={`flex-1 h-px ${i < currentStepIndex ? 'bg-purple-500' : 'bg-white/10'}`} />}\n              </React.Fragment>\n            ))}\n          </div>\n        )}\n\n        {/* ---- STEP 1: FORM ---- */}\n        {joinStep === 'form' && (\n          <form onSubmit={handleFormSubmit} className=\"space-y-5\">\n            <div className=\"bg-[#111111] border border-white/[0.06] rounded-2xl p-6 space-y-4\">\n              <h3 <label className=\"block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider mb-1.5\">Nom de l'entreprise *</label>\n                <input type=\"text\" name=\"companyName\" value={formData.companyName} />\n                  <input type=\"url\" name=\"website\" value={formData.website} onChange={handleInputChange} placeholder=\"https://www.monsite.fr\" required\n                    className=\"w-full </div>\n\n              <div>\n                <label className=\"block text-xs text-gray-500 uppercase tracking-wider mb-1.5\">Secteur d'activité *</label>\n                <select name=\"sector\"  <h3 className=\"text-lg font-bold text-white flex items-center gap-2 mb-2\"><UserIcon size={18} className=\"text-purple-400\" /> Contact référent</h3>\n              <div className=\"grid grid-cols-2 className=\"w-full py-3.5 bg-gradient-to-r from-purple-500 to-violet-600 hover:from-purple-600 hover:to-violet-700 disabled:opacity-40 disabled:cursor-not-allowed text-white font-bold rounded-2xl flex (\n                <div className=\"space-y-6\">\n                  <div className={`w-24 h-24 mx-auto rounded-full ${auditScore >= 50 ? 'bg-yellow-500/10 border-yellow-500/20' : 'bg-orange-500/10 border-orange-500/20'} border-2 flex items-center justify-center`}>\n                    <span className={`text-3xl font-bold ${getScoreColor(auditScore)}`}>{auditScore}</span>\n                  </div>\n                  <div>\n                    <h3 className=\"text-xl font-bold text-white mb-1\">Score AEO : <span className={getScoreColor(auditScore)}>{auditScore}/100</span></h3>\n                    <p className=\"text-gray-500 text-sm\">\n                      {auditScore >= 50 ? 'Votre site a un potentiel AEO intéressant.' : 'Votre site a un fort potentiel d\\'amélioration AEO.'}\n                    </p>\n                  </div>\n\n                  <div className=\"grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 text-left max-w-sm mx-auto\">\n                    {[\n                      { label: 'Schema.org', score: Math.max(10, auditScore - 15 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 10)) },\n                      { label: 'Contenu IA', score: Math.max(10, auditScore - 5 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 15)) },\n                      { label: 'Technique', score: Math.max(20, auditScore + Math.floor(Math.random() * 20)) },\n                      { label: 'Autorité', score: Math.max(15, auditScore - 10 + Math.floor(Math.random() * 10)) },\n                    ].map(cat => (\n                      <div key={cat.label} className=\"p-3 bg-white/[0.03] border border-white/[0.06] rounded-xl\">\n                        <div className=\"flex justify-between items-center mb-1.5\">\n                          <span className=\"text-xs text-gray-500\">{cat.label}</span>\n                          <span className={`text-xs font-bold ${getScoreColor(cat.score)}`}>{cat.score}%</span>\n                        </div>\n                        <div className=\"h-1 bg-white/10 rounded-full overflow-hidden\">\n                          <div className={`h-full rounded-full
